Commercial News

Finance 170

The Gold Market Slightly Weakens 171

There is talk that cash shipments north have been returned. Yesterday, on the 8th, the gold market experienced some fluctuations, with a generally weakening trend, fluctuating by two or three taels. From noon onwards, the total difference was seven taels, resulting in a slightly inferior result of one tael. Each exchange house took its own course, while sentiment was hesitant and uncertain. The silver market's slight decline was not taken seriously. In addition, rising U.S. stocks opened lower. Soon after, foreign exchange both domestically and abroad was tight. Sterling was at 12.9375, and the price turned advantageous, increasing by four or five taels. Suddenly, it was reported that cash shipments to other ports from Tianjin and other banks had been returned due to obstruction. As the news spread, the market price quickly fell sharply, causing a storm. Sellers became aggressive and broke the 50-tael mark. Later, because the exchange rate stabilized, prices rebounded. As the market approached the weekend close, conditions shifted from weak to strong. The difference between the highest and lowest prices of the week was 20 taels, with a total rebound of 10 taels.

The Silver Price Slightly Decreases Before Rebounding After Opening Lower. The market opened lower this morning, decreasing by two taels to 750 taels and eight qian. Large bars and silver prices were each 1/8 lower, but private telegraphs dropped by 5/16, immediately rising to 54.5 taels. Dada Cheng and Hengxing Yuan bought in, and the Bank of China and Japanese banks sold forward three-cent bonds and near-term two-cent bonds at .9375. Later, Wansing, Yuanheng, Shunli Yuanmao Yong, and others sold, immediately causing a drop of more than two taels to 52 taels and three qian. The opening order had already been placed at a small 125, with the U.S. dollar at 2.5 jiao and the Japanese dollar increased by 1.5 fen, at 53 taels and eight qian. Then it added five liang and one qian, and then lowered it again by seven or eight qian.

Various Exchanges Rush to Increase Prices by Two Taels. Da De Cheng, Yi Yu, Fuxing Yong, Xie Xing Yong, Richang, and others bought in, and due to interbank trading of sterling at .9375, various exchanges rushed to sell. The price for the 90th month was the same at .9375, so the gold price immediately rose by two taels to 55 taels and eight qian. Later, due to a sudden rumor that spot goods could not be issued, people were frightened. Major players sold off aggressively, such as Yuanmao Yong, Hengyu, Zhifeng Yong, Cuichang Yong, and the Dalian banks. At 10:30, it was only 50 taels. Not long after, it rose back to 12 taels because Yuanxing Yong, Yifeng Yong, Yuanchun, and others bought, at 52 taels and one qian. At 10:45, sellers suddenly became active, and sterling was sold to banks for three cents, causing another drop of three taels and several qian to 48 taels and a half at 11:00. Then, Yongfeng, the Dalian banks, Yuancheng, and others bought in, and Indian exchange reported a small two annas, resuming customs clearance. At 11:30, it was 51 taels and nine qian.

The Afternoon Results Return a Small One Tael. In an instant, it returned to 50 taels and six or seven qian. Small households sold off. Then, day traders bought to cover their positions, so the market closed at 51 taels and eight qian at noon, then decreasing again to around 51 taels. Compared to the previous day, it had fallen by one tael (according to the official price). The maximum price during the half-day was 55 taels and eight qian, and the minimum price was 48 taels and a half, a difference of seven taels and three qian.

Red Bars are Obstructed, and Sales Prices Decline. Early market price for goods was 51 taels and two qian, up 1.5 taels at noon. The posted price was changed to 798 taels and six qian, a decrease of 45 to 50 taels. The market closed at 47 taels at noon, with ledger entries at 50 to 51 taels and water top-ups at 50 taels. Due to transportation obstructions from Tianjin, Dalian, and other banks, spot red bars were temporarily halted in sales, causing prices to decline, only adding 11 taels. Yingfeng Heng had received 5,000 taels and sold several hundred taels to the Hankou banks.

Different Exchanges Have Different Trading Targets. The trading targets of various exchanges are different. Statistics show that Da De Cheng, Yuanxing Yong, Fuxing Yong, Xie Xing Yong, Fuyu, and others all bought in. Cuichang Yong, Fuchang, Yuanheng, Hengyu, Hengxing Yuan, Futai Heng, and others bought and then sold. Yuanmao Yong, Shunli, Zhifeng Yong, Wanxing, Yuantai, Yuancheng, Tongtaichang, and Tongfeng Heng all sold. Yifeng Yong sold early and then bought. Daxing Yong, Yuanchun, Fushun, Senchang Yong, Taifengcheng, Yongde, and others bought and sold intermittently. Mr. Wu continued to sell. The Dalian banks sold a total of 3,500 to 3,600 bars and only bought 500 to 600 bars. The Guangdong banks had no transactions.

Yarn and Cotton Market Still Difficult to Be Optimistic 177

The yarn market is showing a fluctuating pattern again, which is expected after a large drop. However, the overall situation remains weak and sluggish. The severe flooding in various regions has greatly reduced purchasing power, business is sluggish, and all routes are completely stagnant. People are increasingly softening, and large households are still selling, putting heavy pressure on the market. In short, the situation in the world cotton industry is still difficult to be optimistic about. However, the bulls hope that the gold market will rise again. Unfortunately, natural and man-made disasters are coming one after another, and autumn sales will inevitably be reduced. The future depends on actual demand.

Slight Shortage of Bidders, Exchange Bidding Market Opens: The exchange bidding market opened, and the sentiment was slightly firm due to the stability of American cotton. There was a slight shortage of sellers in the market, and prices for all months rose by 2, 3, 5, and 6 cents. The afternoon market was flat, and some large households sold, causing near-term prices to fall by 2 cents and far-term prices to rise by 1 or 2 cents. The total transaction volume was 26,300 bales. It was found that 1,750 bales were sold by Ruida, 1,950 bales by Yichang, 450 bales by Mingde, 400 bales by Gongtai, 400 bales by Xiesheng, and 400 bales by Shenxin. 1,350 bales were bought by No. 20, 600 bales by Shengtai, 950 bales by Yida, and 550 bales by Dafu. There is concern about the possibility of disturbances. The whole city has news of rising prices, so more people are increasing their purchases. However, the overall global situation and the past consumption of U.S. cotton have not escaped the dire situation, so the large households are still shorting, and the outlook is still mostly bearish.

Grains: Rice Market Rising Sharply 183

South City: No ships from various groups arrived, the amount in the warehouse is also scarce, retail sales in urban and rural stores are sluggish, and foreign rice has risen to nearly one yuan, causing public panic. The price of thick japonica rice has risen sharply by 60 to 70 cents. The sales of thin indica rice on this street are slightly better, causing the price to continue to rise by about 50 cents. Luxiang pointed rice is scarce and dry, and the market price has followed up by 20 to 30 cents. Yinhua Yuantong has become a broken chain, and sales are tight again. Foreign rice is still sporadic, and re-exports are particularly active. The market shape is showing a surprising peak due to the high production price.

New Gate: Yesterday, the Social Bureau publicly evaluated prices in the Cuixiutang public office in the City God Temple, and all prices in Hexia were opened. Traders are unwilling to open the market due to capital losses. However, the public association did not open Changxi and Beigeng rice and thin indica rice due to the small price limit, but the merchants directly opened prices, and there were also transactions. The unified market opening was limited, and the prices of various goods were stabilized.

Wheat Prices Rise, Flour Market Soars 184

Yesterday, the flour market suddenly soared due to the surge in wheat prices by 70 to 90 cents. There was also a telegram about the United States dumping wheat to Germany. Generally, people speculate that if U.S. wheat is shipped to Europe, the quantity coming to China will inevitably decrease. Domestic floods are frequent, and rice prices are also rising, so it stimulated people's hearts and they rushed to buy. Moreover, the various groups in the Yangtze River in the interior have always been bullish. With this opportunity, they inevitably raised prices. The highest prices in each month were more than 30 cents higher than the previous day. Later, due to the release of goods from Tianjin, the amount was not small, and it was reported that there was a fixed price for foreign flour there, with a straight price of 3 taels, 1 qian, and 6 fen, so the sentiment slightly calmed down. As a result, the price for the current month rose by 17.5 cents compared to the previous day, the price for September rose by 25 cents, the price for October and November rose by 22.5 cents, and the price for December and January rose by 20 cents.

Wheat Price Soars by Over 10 Cents 185

Yesterday, the wheat futures market suddenly showed a soaring trend because foreign wheat prices soared by a huge 70, 80, or 90 cents. It was rumored that U.S. wheat was being shipped to Europe, and it was about to become a reality, so everyone suspected that future wheat orders would be hopeless. With the continuous disasters in the country, domestic wheat prices must be expensive, so buying was unusually active, and market prices soared. Although factories were still selling, it was like a drop in the bucket and did not help. As a result, the price for the current month rose by 70 cents compared to the previous day, the price for September rose by 80 cents, the price for October and November rose by 90 cents, and the price for December rose by a huge 100 cents. In the spot wheat market, the sentiment has become strong due to the surge in standard wheat. High-quality goods have already opened at 80 cents, and even lower quality goods are above 60 cents. The future looks promising. It is said that more than 3,000 bales of Kunshan, Taicang, Shuangfeng, Zhitang, and Penglai wheat were opened and handled by Fuxin Huafeng.

As a result, Harmony, Jardine, and other companies with large sales have become more interested in purchasing. Chinese merchants are also taking the opportunity to hoard the tea in their hands.
